development ordinance 1  land development ordinance general provisions 11  title and intent a this ordinance governs the conversion of raw land and parcels into subdivided tracts and lots for the construction of buildings and other structures and development and shall be known as the land development the city of hanahan sc herein referred to as the land development  b the purpose of this ordinance is to provide for harmonious orderly and progressive development of land to promote the public health safety economy good order appearance convenience and general welfare of the citizens of hanahan this purpose shall be achieved following objectives c encouraging the development of an economically sound and stable city  1 assuring in general the wise and timely development of new areas or redevelopment of areas in harmony with the comprehensive plan  2 assuring the timely provision of required streets utilities and other facilities and services to new development of land  3 assuring safe and convenient traffic access and circulation  both vehicular and pedestrian  in and development projects  and 4 assuring the provision of needed public open spaces and building sites in new development projects by dedication or reservation of land for recreation education transportation and other public purposes d purpose south carolina sets forth five 5 purposes for municipal regulation of land development restated below following these are additional purposes established by the city of hanahan to uphold and promote the public health safety economy good order appearance convenience morals and general welfare scc  6291120 the hanahan planning commission is charged with the implementation of these purposes in part review and approval of preliminary land development plans for major land developments and minor land development plats 1 encourage the development of an economically sound and stable city 2 assure the timely provision of required streets utilities and other facilities and services to new development of land 3 assure the adequate provision of safe and convenient traffic access and circulation both vehicular and pedestrian in and land developments 4 assure the provision of needed public open spaces and building sites in new land developments dedication or reservation of land for recreational educational transportation and other public purposes 5 assure in general the wise and timely development of new areas and redevelopment of previously developed areas in harmony with the hanahan comprehensive plan 6 assure the development of new areas in a manner and arrangement that minimizes impacts on sensitive and valued resources such as landmark trees wetland ecosystems and water quality avoidance of natural features and progressive stormwater management 7 assure the integration and accessibility of new public spaces  streets sidewalks parks school sites and the like  into the existing built environment of hanahan sensitive urban design 12  policy a it is declared to be the policy of the city of hanahan to consider the subdivision of land and development thereof as subject to the control of the city pursuant to the adopted comprehensive plan for the orderly planned efficient and economical development of hanahan b land subdivided shall be of such character that it can be used safely for building purposes without danger to health or peril from fire flood or other menace and land shall not be subdivided until adequate public facilities and improvements exist and proper provision has been made for drainage water sewerage and capital improvements such as schools parks recreational facilities transportation facilities and other improvements c the existing and proposed public improvements shall conform to and be properly related to the policies of the comprehensive plan official zoning map and capital budget and program of the city and it is intended that these regulations shall supplement and facilitate the enforcement of the provisions and standards contained in building and housing codes the zoning the comprehensive plan and the capital budget and program d land that has been subdivided prior to the effective date of these regulations should whenever possible be brought within the scope of these regulations to further the purposes of standards identified in 3  jurisdiction a this ordinance is adopted pursuant to the authority granted under  6291110 of the laws of south carolina the hanahan planning commission is vested with the authority to review approve conditionally approve and disapprove applications for the subdivision and development of land b these regulations apply to all subdivision and development of land located within the corporate limits of the city of hanahan the planning commission may grant modifications of these regulations pursuant to the provisions of c no land may be subdivided use of any legal description other than with reference to a plat approved by the planning commission andor the city planner in accordance with these regulations 14  severability should any portion of this ordinance be found illegal by a court of competent jurisdiction the remainder of the ordinance shall remain in effect 15  amendments for the purpose of protecting the public health safety and general welfare the planning commission may from time to time propose amendments to these regulations which shall then be approved or disapproved by city council following the amendment procedure set forth in of the zoning enforcement a in general no grading or excavation of land or construction of any public or private improvements shall commence in violation with the provisions of these ordinances no land described in this section shall be subdivided sold leased or transferred until the developer has filed a final plat approved by the hanahan city planner or planning commission with the berkeley county register of deeds no zoning or building permit or certificate of occupancy shall be issued for any lot or parcel of land or any building or structure located thereon that is subdivided developed or sold in violation of the hanahan zoning and land development ordinances the city of hanahan shall have no obligation to issue a certificate of occupancy or to extend utility services to any parcel created in violation of these ordinances b interpretation terms used in this ordinance shall have the meaning specified in terms  of the hanahan zoning the ordinances are mute the term shall have its regular dictionary definition c limit on reapplication except for requests which are continued with the mutual consent of the applicant and the planning commission an applicant shall not initiate duplicate application for land development affecting the same parcel of property or any part thereof more often than once in twelve 12 months d violations 1 the city planner as provided in shall be empowered to utilize all of the enforcement tools provided to the zoning administrator per the hanahan zoning 2 the city planner may deny administrative land development approval andor withhold a land disturbance permit as he deems necessary to ensure compliance with the hanahan land development developer may appeal such action to the hanahan planning commission per 7  city planner a the office of the city planner shall be charged with the administration and enforcement of the hanahan land development which shall entail the following duties 1 interpreting the land development   2 administering permits and approvals  3 processing applications for plan and plat review  4 fee collection for permits and plan and plat review  5 processing appeals to the planning commission and preparing the record for appeal to circuit court  6 maintaining public records related to land development  7 investigating and resolving complaints pertaining to the ordinance  8 enforcing the ordinance  and 9 other duties as may be assigned b the city administrator may designate the zoning administrator provided for in of the hanahan zoning as the city planner if the city planner and the zoning administrator are two 2 separate individuals the zoning administrator shall be authorized to assist the city planner with administration and enforcement of the hanahan land development general procedure a applicability whenever a person proposes the adjustment or subdivision of the land vacant or improved involving two 2 or more lots for the purpose of offer sale lease or development approval by the city planner andor the planning commission shall be required in addition to all other procedures and approvals required in the zoning whether or not applicable zoning procedures also require approval review or recommendation all such proposals are herein referred to as land developments b classification of land developments before any changing of land characteristics construction subdivision into parcels condominium complexes commercial parks shopping centers industrial parks mobile home parks and similar developments for sale lease or any combination of owner and rental characteristics the owners of such properties or their authorized agent shall apply for and secure approval of the proposed land development in accordance with the procedures provided herein a proposal shall be classified as one 1 of the following types c exempt subdivision certain land developments are exempt from planning commission review and approval per south carolina 2 as amended and shall be submitted to the city planner for information prior to recordation with berkeley county the city planner shall stamp at least one 1 submitted plat as received and exempt so that the applicant may submit the plat to berkeley county for recordation the criteria for exempt subdivisions are as follows 1 the combination or recombination of portions of previously platted lots where the total number of lots is not increased and the resultant lots are equal to city standards sometimes referred to as a boundary line adjustment 2 the combination or recombination of entire lots of record where no new street or change in existing streets is involved 3 the division of land into parcels of five 5 acres or more where no new street is involved d record drawing a record drawing is the depiction of the survey of an existing lot typically performed prior to property transfer for purposes of the hanahan land development record drawings shall be subject to the same standards as exempt subdivisions e criticalarea delineation a criticalarea delineation is the survey of critical area consisting entirely of wetlands regulated by the state of south carolina a criticalarea delineation shall not create any new parcels and shall merely reestablish wetlands boundaries in some cases the boundaries of existing parcels may be reestablished where adjacent to tidal marsh creeks and drainage rightsofway for purposes of the hanahan land development criticalarea delineations shall be subject to the same standards as exempt subdivisions f minor land development subdivision of land resulting in the alteration or creation of five 5 or fewer parcels totaling less than one 1 acre neither requiring or resulting in the installation of new or upgraded infrastructure described in this ordinance whether privately or publicly maintained including transportation stormwater management and other systems shall be a minor land development 1 a remnant parcel five 5 acres or more in size with street frontage meeting city standards to remain in its predeveloped state and requiring and resulting in no additional infrastructure need not contribute to the oneacre or fiveparcel standards 2 the planning commission may require the developer of a minor land development due to its complexity or unusual conditions to pursue major land development review and approval g major land development 1 any land development requiring or resulting in the installation of new or upgraded infrastructure including but not limited to transportation stormwater management potable water and sanitary sewerage infrastructure shall be a major land development 2 any subdivision of land not classified a minor land development shall be a major land development 19  modification of land development standards a where the planning commission finds that extraordinary hardships derived from practical difficulties may result from strict compliance with these regulations andor that the purposes of these regulations may be served to a greater extent by an alternative proposal it may approve modifications to these land development regulations so that substantial justice may be done and the public interest secured provided that the modification does not have the effect of nullifying the intent and purpose of these regulations  further provided the planning commission shall not approve modifications unless it makes findings based upon the evidence presented to it in each specific case that all of the following criteria apply 1 the granting of the modification will not be detrimental to the public safety health or welfare or injurious to other property  2 the conditions upon which the request is based are unique to the property for which the relief is sought and are not applicable generally to other property  3 because of the particular physical surroundings shape or topographical conditions of the specific property involved a particular hardship to the owner would result  as distinguished from a mere inconvenience  if the strict letter of these regulations is carried out  and 4 the modification sought will not in any manner be in conflict with the provisions of zoning standards of this ordinance or the policies of the comprehensive plan b procedure the planning commission shall be empowered to modify land development standards in the course of land development review and approval the developer shall bear the responsibility to demonstrate to the planning commission that the modification sought meets the criteria for modification stated above the procedure shall be that provided for appeals to the planning commission in of this ordinance c conditions in allowing modifications the planning commission may require such conditions as will in its judgment secure substantially the intent and policies described in this chapter d documentation upon granting or allowing a modification the planning commission shall then state in writing findings of fact supporting its decision to grant or allow the modification 110  appeals of decisions of the city planner on land development applications a procedure for appeal an applicant or any party of legal standing believing to have found error in the written decision of the city planner may appeal the decision to the planning commission 1 appeal submittal ten 10 copies of the application in question shall be submitted to the city planner not less than twentyfive 25 days prior to the meeting at which it is to be considered by the planning commission 2 application and fee the appellant shall file an appeal by completing the form available from the city planner and submit it together with an application fee in an amount set by hanahan city council the appellant shall state on the form reasons for the appeal the date of receipt of the completed application shall be the official submittal date and stamped by the city planner on the completed written appeal as received b city procedure the planning commission shall act on the submitted appeal within sixty 60 days of the official submittal date failure to act within sixty 60 days shall constitute automatic approval and the appellant shall be notified of this in writing the sixtyday time limit may be extended by mutual agreement between the appellant and the city planner 1 notification of meeting action taken by the planning commission on the appeal shall be at a scheduled public meeting and notice of the time and place of said meeting shall be mailed by the city to the appellant such notice shall be sent not less than fifteen 15 days before the date of the meeting conspicuous notices shall be posted on or adjacent to the affected property by the city planner one notice shall be visible from each transportation rightofway that borders the property at least fifteen 15 days prior to the public meeting 2 decision of the planning commission the concurring vote of the majority of members of the commission shall be necessary to reverse any order requirement decision or determination of the city planner upon decision of the planning commission three 3 copies of the plat shall be retained by the city for its records and the remaining copies returned to the applicant one 1 of which shall be signed by the chairperson of the planning commission and the city planner and bearing the date of approval or disapproval with written reasons for such action attached c an applicant or any party of legal standing may appeal a decision of the planning commission to circuit court filing with the clerk of such court a petition in writing setting forth plainly fully and distinctly wherein such decision is contrary to law the applicant must appeal within thirty 30 days of receiving written notice of the decision 111  vested rights to develop property   definitions a except as hereinafter set forth the words terms and phrases when used in this shall have the meaning as set forth in of the south carolina laws as enacted by act 287 of 2004 b the following actions and documents approved or issued by the city planner zoning administrator planning commission board of zoning appeals design control committee and city council shall constitute authorization of a sitespecific development plan 1 planned development district type b including master development plan 2 preliminary land development plan 3 land disturbance permit 4 final plat 5 site development plan 6 zoning permit 7 zoning variance 8 special exception 9 certificate of appropriateness   establishment and conditions of vested rights a a vested right to developer property in accordance with a sitespecific development plan is triggered upon the final approval of the sitespecific development plan by the final official or body of the municipality authorized to approve the sitespecific development plan and the payment to the city of all applicable established fees b except as hereinafter set forth a vested right established by this is subject to the conditions and limitations as set out in  6291540 and 6291550 of the laws of south carolina as enacted by act 287 of 2004 c a vested right for an approved sitespecific development plan expires two 2 years after the date of final approval by the final official or body authorized to approve a sitespecific development plan d when approved with conditions the sitespecific development plan shall not confer vested rights unless the conditions of approval have been met the vesting period shall nevertheless commence upon the date of conditional approval e no vested rights are established for phased development plans including approved or conditionally approved phased development plans and including phased development plans applicable to property proposed for annexation an approved or conditionally approved sitespecific development plan is required prior to approval with respect to each phase of a phased development plan f a vested sitespecific development plan may be amended if the amendment conforms to or does not cause greater nonconformity with the then current provisions of hanahan zoning and land development ordinances approval or conditional approval of an amendment does not reset or restart the expiration period of a vested right g no sooner than three 3 months and no later than fortyfive 45 days prior to the expiration of the twoyear vested right period for an approved sitespecific development plan the landowner of the property with a vested right in a sitespecific development plan may apply to the zoning administrator for a zoning and design authorization or to the city planner for a land development authorization for an annual extension of the vested right the authorized official must approve an application for an annual extension of the vested right unless an amendment to the hanahan zoning or land development been adopted that prohibits approval no more than five 5 annual extensions of the vested right may be approved 2  land development application and review process 21  intent of chapter the following steps constitute the land development approval process for projects in city of hanahan each step is required unless stated otherwise 22  preapplication conference the developer is strongly encouraged but not required to participate in a preapplication conference with the hanahan city planner before applying to the city of hanahan for approval of a land development or planned development district the developer should contact the city planner to arrange an appointment to discuss a project proposal the developer should bring a sketch plan of the proposed land development or pdd master plan to facilitate the discussion  purpose the preapplication conference provides the city planner the opportunity to a determine whether the land development is an exempt subdivision minor land development or major land development b familiarize the developer with the land development approval process of the city of hanahan  c assess the compatibility of the proposed land development with the hanahan comprehensive plan  and d apprise the developer of city state and federal standards related to the development of land and their potential applicability to the developers proposal including but not limited to 1 hanahan land development design and improvements standards of this ordinance  2 standards of the hanahan zoning   3 standards of the hanahan flood damage prevention   4 berkeley county land development and engineering standards for roads and drainage  5 berkeley county water and sanitation authority standards for potable water provision and sanitary sewerage  6 state standards for roads and encroachments as administrated by the department of transportation  7 state standards for onsite sewage disposal as promulgated by the department of health and environmental control  8 state standards for wetlands protection stormwater management erosion and sedimentation reduction as promulgated by the office of ocean and coastal resources management  9 federal standards for wetlands and water quality protection as promulgated by us army corps of engineers  and 10 federal standards for endangered species protection as administrated by the south carolina department of natural resources  procedure the city planner shall review any provided sketch plan with the developer the city planner may suggest that the developer submit the sketch plan to the planning commission for comment and recommendation should the developer voluntarily agree to submit to the planning commission the following procedures shall apply a the developer shall submit the sketch plan to the city planner at least fifteen 15 days before a regularly scheduled meeting of the planning commission so that the city planner can distribute the document to the planning commission with appropriate research and commentary b this service is provided free of charge to the developer and no formal application is required  however the sketch plan should include those items specified in of this ordinance c the city planner shall include the sketch plan as an agenda item on the next regularly scheduled planning commission meeting d the city planner should draft a report to the planning commission as to the compatibility of the sketch plan with the comprehensive plan and as to the compliance of applicable zoning standards e the planning commission shall review the sketch plan for compatibility with the comprehensive plan and may vote to approve conditionally approve or disapprove the sketch plan f the planning commission may include as conditions any recommendations it has to uphold and promote the objectives of the comprehensive plan  approval nonbinding the vote on the sketch plan is advisory only to the developer and does not prevent him from applying for any land development approval likewise sketch plan approval does not authorize the developer to commence in any land disturbance improvements or other land development activities the developer is strongly encouraged to resubmit after two 2 years if no further land development approval process steps are taken 23  preliminary land development plan  applicability a the preliminary plan is the first required step in the major land development approval process b a developer proposing an exempt subdivision or a minor land development need not submit a preliminary plan only the developer proposing a major land development must apply for planning commission review and approval of a preliminary plan  purpose a the hanahan planning commission is charged with the implementation of the purposes of land development regulations specified in of this ordinance in part review and approval of preliminary plans for major land developments b the developer shall demonstrate to the planning commission the intent and ability to meet or exceed all zoning and land development standards of the city of hanahan c approval or conditional approval of a preliminary plan authorizes the developer to begin engineering and construction drawings for community facilities needed for land development  procedure a the developer shall submit a preliminary plan to the city planner no fewer than twentyfive 25 days before the planning commission meeting at which he seeks plan approval b the city planner shall date and stamp the preliminary plan received c a complete preliminary land development plan includes those items specified in of this ordinance which include but are not limited to an application form and fee d notification of meeting the city planner shall notify the developer of the time and place of the planning commission meeting at which the land development is to be considered no fewer than five 5 days before the meeting at which the preliminary plan is to be considered a copy of the agenda for the meeting shall suffice as written notice e decision on preliminary land development plan 1 the planning commission shall approve approve conditionally or disapprove the preliminary plan at its regularly scheduled monthly meeting or at a duly advertised called meeting 2 the planning commission may attach conditions of approval that uphold and promote the purposes of land development regulations stated in the commission shall have the authority to require changes to preliminary plans as conditions of approval in order to uphold and promote those purposes changes may relate to land development content arrangement and design the commission may modify land development regulations as they apply to the preliminary land development plan under review provided those same purposes are upheld and promoted standards for modification appear in the commission shall not require or allow modified zoning standards unless authorized to do so in specific cases as provided in the hanahan 3 the planning commission shall act on the preliminary plan within sixty 60 days of the official submittal date failure to act within sixty 60 days shall constitute automatic approval and the developer shall be notified in writing the sixtyday time limit may be extended by mutual agreement between the developer and the city planner 4 the city planner shall submit to the developer a written report of the planning commissions decision with any attached conditions of approval or reasons for disapproval within ten 10 days of the decision 24  land disturbance permit the developer shall be eligible to apply for a land disturbance permit after gaining planning commission approval of a preliminary land development plan and meeting any attached conditions  purpose a the land disturbance permit is the enforcement tool by which the city planner can assure that a major land development is constructed in accordance with the preliminary plan approval or conditional approval and furthermore that the land development will meet or exceed the design and improvements standards for community facilities specified in of this ordinance b the developer shall demonstrate upon application for a land disturbance permit achievement of federal state and local natural resource protection standards during construction and the ability to meet natural resource protection standards during construction and postconstruction c this step allows the developer to avoid the potential costs of significant changes to engineering drawings required by the planning commission during its review of the preliminary plan d receipt of a land disturbance permit authorizes the developer to clear and grade land remove trees in accordance with hanahan tree protection standards of the zoning  and install community improvements  procedure a the developer shall submit to the city planner a completed application for a land disturbance permit which the city planner shall date and stamp received b a completed application for a land disturbance permit includes those items specified in of this ordinance which include but are not limited to an application form and fee c the city planner shall have no more than thirty 30 days in which to review the completed application and either issue the land disturbance permit or submit to the developer in writing reasons for disapproval the city planner shall be authorized to inspect natural resource protection measures proposed as part of the land development as applicable the thirtyday time limit may be extended by mutual agreement between the developer and the city planner d the developer shall post an approved land disturbance permit on the major land development site at a location easily visible and accessible from the adjacent transportation rightofway until improvements specified in the application for the permit are installed pass inspection of and are where applicable successfully dedicated to the appropriate agency e the developer may appeal the decision of the city planner to the planning commission in accordance with the appeals process specified in 5  thirdparty review and inspection the developer may propose improvements that do not meet berkeley county standards for engineering construction development and stormwater drainage adopted by the city of hanahan by reference as land development design and improvements standards this option shall only be available where alternate standards are provided in the following standards shall apply a the developer shall designate a professional engineer approved by the city planner who is not employed by the developer or any firm hired by the developer or any subcontractor thereof for the proposed land development under consideration to review the land development plans and inspect their construction to a standard equivalent to the detail and frequency of berkeley county inspectors the city planner may require more detailed or frequent inspections where necessary to ensure compliance with the intent of this ordinance and to uphold good engineering practices as promulgated by recognized professional resources such as the aashto green book b the fees of thirdparty review for various engineers shall appear in the city of hanahan schedule of fees and fines and made available to the developer upon request the fees shall be percentages of construction costs of the improvements subject to thirdparty review or other quantifiable dollar amount based on the size or extent of the land development or system of improvements proposed c the developer shall indicate to the city planner in writing his desire to utilize the services of the selected thirdparty engineer and submit to the city planner upon application for land disturbance permit an itemized construction costs estimate of those improvements proposed for thirdparty review the written notification shall commit the developer to the selected engineer for the duration of the land development process or phase thereof and shall indicate acceptance of responsibility for fees d the amount of fees shall be altered only if 1 the land disturbance permit is expired or up for renewal or 2 the city planner finds or learns from the thirdparty engineer that the developer miscalculated construction costs upon renewal of a land disturbance permit the developer shall recalculate and submit a new construction costs estimate and may choose another engineer for thirdparty review miscalculation of construction costs shall be a violation of this ordinance which if not corrected by the developer shall authorize the city planner to take enforcement action e a change from the thirdparty engineer originally selected during construction document review or inspection shall be approved solely by the city planner who shall document in writing that good cause exists for the change such as unprofessional conduct or unexpected unavailability of the thirdparty engineer the developer shall then select a replacement approved by the city planner f the thirdparty professional engineer shall report to the city planner in writing his conclusions as to whether alternative plans further the objectives of this ordinance and his findings upon inspection of improvements under construction as to the successful implementation of approved plans the city planner shall forward written reports to the developer who shall address any deficiencies in the report to the satisfaction of the thirdparty engineer and the city planner g the city of hanahan not the developer shall be responsible for payment of the thirdparty engineer 26  field changes onsite conditions may unduly inhibit land development and as depicted in an approved or conditionally approved preliminary land development plan andor the successful land disturbance permit application in this event the developer shall submit any changes to the preliminary plan or the land disturbance permit application to the city planner for review and approval field changes shall meet the following standards a all land development standards of the city of hanahan shall apply or the developer may seek modification of standards per b the field change shall be sufficiently minor as deemed by the city planner field changes that result in a significant change typically ten 10 percent or greater in the quantity or extent of lots community facilities or affected natural resources shall require the developer to resubmit the amended preliminary land development plan for planning commission review and approval c the developer shall submit a request in writing for a field change to the city planner which the city planner shall date and stamp received d the city planner shall have fifteen 15 days from the date of receipt to review the field change and respond in writing to the developer the city planner shall approve the field change or instruct the developer to resubmit for preliminary land development plan approval the fifteenday time limit may be extended by mutual agreement between the developer and the city planner 27  final plat the developer shall be eligible to apply for final plat approval after receipt of a land disturbance permit and completion or assurance of completion of all public andor common improvements indicated in the approved preliminary land development plan  purpose a an approved final plat enables the developer to subdivide property into lots for transfer or to seek a zoning permit for use b the final plat shall conform in all respects to the approved preliminary plan as amended to meet attached conditions and as amended by field changes c the city planner approves a final plat only after the developer has satisfactorily completed all public andor private community facilities such as systems of infrastructure sites for public buildings and common open space alternatively the developer may financially guarantee completion of the improvements per d final plat approval does not constitute acceptance of existing or proposed community facilities the developer shall make arrangements for the maintenance of community facilities per e final plat approval shall be a prerequisite for a zoning permit for any lot proposed in the land development  procedure a the developer shall submit a final plat to the city planner who shall date and stamp the final plat received b a complete final plat includes those items specified in of this ordinance which include but are not limited to an application form and fee c the city planner shall have no more than thirty 30 days in which to review and either approve or disapprove the final plat the city planner shall be authorized to inspect community facilities natural resource protection measures and landscaping proposed as part of the land development as applicable the city planner shall then sign and date the approved final plat for recordation or submit in writing reasons for disapproval to the developer the thirtyday time limit may be extended by mutual agreement between the developer and the city planner d the developer may appeal the decision of the city planner to the planning commission in accordance with the appeals process specified in  recordation of plat the city planner shall retain one 1 copy of the final plat for city of hanahan records and return remaining copies to the developer the developer shall be responsible for filing the final plat with the berkeley county register of deeds 28  minor land development plat the developer shall be eligible to apply for minor land development plat approval for a proposal that that qualifies as a minor land development per f of this ordinance  purpose and applicability a the hanahan planning commission is charged with the implementation of the purposes of land development regulations specified in of this ordinance in part review and approval of plats for minor land developments b the developer shall demonstrate to the planning commission the intent and ability to meet or exceed all zoning and land development standards of the city of hanahan c the minor land development plat is equivalent to a final plat submitted to the planning commission for review and approval of minor land development d approval of a minor land development plat authorizes the developer subdivide the land into lots for transfer or to seek a zoning permit for use  procedure a the developer shall submit a minor land development plat to the city planner no fewer than twentyfive 25 days before the planning commission meeting at which he seeks plan approval b the city planner shall date and stamp the plat received c a complete minor land development plat includes those items specified for a final plat in of this ordinance which include but are not limited to an application form and fee d notification of meeting the city planner shall notify the developer of the time and place of the planning commission meeting at which the land development is to be considered no fewer than five 5 days before the meeting at which the minor land development plat is to be considered a copy of the agenda for the meeting shall suffice as written notice e decision on minor land development plat 1 the planning commission shall approve approve conditionally or disapprove the minor land development plat at its regularly scheduled monthly meeting or at a duly advertised called meeting 2 the planning commission may attach conditions of approval that uphold and promote the purposes of land development regulations stated in the commission shall have the authority to require changes to minor land development plats as conditions of approval in order to uphold and promote those purposes changes may relate to land development content arrangement and design the commission may modify land development regulations as they apply to the minor land development plat under review provided those same purposes are upheld and promoted standards for modification appear in the commission shall not require or allow modified zoning standards unless authorized to do so in specific cases as provided in the hanahan 3 the planning commission shall act on the minor land development plat within sixty 60 days of the official submittal date failure to act within sixty 60 days shall constitute automatic approval and the city planner shall notify the developer of this in writing the sixtyday time limit may be extended by mutual agreement between the developer and the city planner 4 the city planner shall submit to the developer a written report of the planning commissions decision with any attached conditions of approval or reasons for disapproval within ten 10 days of the decision 5 if the planning commission has approved the minor land development plat and any and all conditions of approval have been met the city planner shall sign and date the approved plat for recordation and submit it to the developer  recordation of plat the city planner shall retain one 1 copy of the minor land development plat for city of hanahan records and return remaining copies to the developer the developer shall be responsible for filing the plat with the berkeley county register of deeds 29  record drawings a a record drawing documents completed improvements required to serve the land development and an asbuilt survey executed by the developer as evidence that all improvements have been installed according to an approved preliminary land development plan and application for land disturbance permit in compliance with design and improvements standards of this ordinance b the developer shall submit one 1 copy of record drawings of all completed improvements upon application for final plat approval all incomplete improvements shall be financially guaranteed per record drawings of financially guaranteed improvements shall be submitted prior to release of financial guarantees c the developer shall submit copies of record drawings to utility providers expected to maintain the improvements and shall provide verification to the city planner from the utility provider that all improvements have been installed to their specifications prior to final plat approval or release of financial guarantees 210  zoning permit the developer of a building site shall obtain a zoning permit prior to commencing any site development activities including clearing and tree removal performed for and development site preparation of the hanahan zoning for the applicability purpose procedure documentation requirements and appeal process for a zoning permit the developer is strongly encouraged to participate in a preapplication conference per of this ordinance prior to seeking a zoning permit 211  building permit the developer in receipt of a zoning permit shall be eligible to apply for a building permit all standards for review and approval shall be found in the building code adopted by the city of hanahan as amended the application procedure for a building permit shall be that found in of the hanahan zoning a proposals of construction and reconstruction shall secure a building permit from the city of hanahan where such is required by the building code adopted by the city of hanahan as amended except that public utilities installing and repairing transmission lines poles and substations shall be exempt b the purposes of building code administration shall be those found in the building code adopted by the city of hanahan as amended 212  certificate of occupancy a developer or other applicant in receipt of a building permit andor zoning permit shall obtain a certificate of occupancy prior to taking residence or commencing business in the structure for which the permit is received the application procedure for a certificate of occupancy shall be that found in of the hanahan zoning a all public improvements including those financially guaranteed in a major land development shall be completed to the satisfaction of the city of hanahan prior to application for a certificate of occupancy for any structure within the major land development in the event of a phased land development each of these systems shall be completed within the current phase and all previous phases b application for a certificate of occupancy signals to the building official and the zoning administrator that construction and site improvements specified in applications for a building permit and a zoning permit are complete or where allowed are financially guaranteed 213  outline of the approval process for major land ordinance referenced by the section for which he desires more information 3  land development documentation requirements 31  sketch plan this step is strictly voluntary and description of content spelled out for the sketch plan is to provide guidance to the developer a the sketch plan of a proposed land development should be legibly drawn to scale without necessarily showing precise dimensions and should contain at least the following information 1 north arrow  2 written andor graphic scales  3 location map showing the relationship between the proposed development and the surrounding properties  4 tract boundaries and total acreages  5 approximate sizes and locations of existing structures  6 existing and proposed land uses throughout the development  7 existing character of the land such as approximate locations of natural resources which may be identified on aerial photography  8 tentative street and lot arrangement showing average lot size and the number of lots  9 nonresidential sites with approximate acreages and gross floor area where applicable  10 zoning classifications  and 11 designation of phases where applicable b a completed application for sketch plan review should include a form available from the city planner that indicates land ownership and representation where applicable and contact information for both the berkeley county parcel identification numbers and the property address where available of the subject property should be specified on the application form no fee is required since this step is voluntary 32  preliminary land 10 copies of the traffic study where required standards and content requirements for the traffic study appear in b documentation requirements the completed application for preliminary land development across rightsofway e all existing municipal boundaries property lines rightsofway easements railroads water and sewer lines fire hydrants utility transmission lines culverts bridges storm drainage footprints shall indicate intent to meet or exceed any building design regulations promulgated in the hanahan zoning l any required vegetative buffers tree protection areas and tree planting requirements such as street trees and roadside trees 5 platting information a the total tract boundary lines of the area being developed shall be in accordance with the most recent edition of the minimum standards manual for the practice of land surveying in south carolina as promulgated by the laws of south carolina title 40 b the preliminary land development plan shall meet all standards and requirements as set forth in the laws of the state of south carolina and these regulations 6 supplemental data any other information required by ordinance or considered pertinent by the applicant the planning commission or the city planner to the review of the preliminary land development plan shall be submitted with or on the plan 33  traffic study a applicability a traffic study shall be required as part of a complete application for preliminary land development plan approval or zoning permit for any land development projected to generate one hundred 100 or more peakhour vehicle trips at any intersection at the perimeter of the land development the planning commission may request a traffic study in its consideration of a proposed planned development district trip generation rates from the applicable current manual of the institute of transportation engineers or equivalent shall apply b study scope the planning commission may require any or all of the following the city planner should indicate these needs to the applicant prior to the planning commission review of the preliminary land development plan 1 the results of the traffic study may be reported to the planning commission in writing full traffic impact analysis or other means appropriate to the scale of the study as acceptable to the planning commission 2 the traffic study area shall include all existing and proposed road intersections and segments along the perimeter of the land development site the planning commission may also require the study to include road intersections and segments of collector and arterial roads that provide direct access to the land development site 3 periods of analysis shall include daily and peakhour traffic 4 analysis scenarios shall include existing conditions and conditions at proposed buildout the planning commission may require intermediate scenarios as well 5 where desired by the planning commission the process for determining trip generation and distribution including generation category and diversion and distribution assumptions shall be reported 6 the study shall include growth rate in background traffic assumptions 7 the study shall include to the extent practical the impacts of nearby land developments with potentially overlapping study areas and proposed transportation system improvements c existing conditions the traffic study shall report existing conditions including 1 graphic representation of the road system with geometric features lane usage signage curb cuts adjacent traffic generators  2 traffic volumes including average daily traffic which may be available from scdot and peakhour traffic which shall be seasonally adjusted eg to account for school traffic to the extent practical  3 capacity of road intersections and segments in the study area  and 4 other information as deemed necessary by the planning commission including but not limited to sight distances queue length analysis pedestrian counts accident data and traffic speeds 50th and 85th percentile d projected future conditions the traffic study shall project future conditions with and without the proposed land development the latter of which shall account for traffic growth rate and completion of approved nearby land developments with potentially overlapping study areas the report shall include the following details of future conditions with the proposed land development 1 projections of daily and peakhour traffic distributed into the road network  2 capacity analysis at buildout and any required intermediate points in time  and 3 where deemed necessary by the planning commission determination of warrants for signalization safe sight distances gap analysis turning radius requirements queue length analysis turning lane length analysis curb cut locations and design speeds with proposed posted speed limits e mitigation plan the traffic study shall conclude with recommendations to add turn lanes traffic signage and signals and other measures to offset negative impacts that exceed capacity or absorb a large proportion typically onethird  13  or more of capacity in an area expected to grow significantly as determined by the planning commission the mitigation plan shall not neglect potential impacts of its recommendations on bicycle and pedestrian access and safety the recommendations of the mitigation plan shall be conditions of preliminary land development plan andor zoning permit approval failure to implement the recommendations shall be grounds for disapproval or denial of a rezoning request 34  land disturbance permit a application requirements the following constitute a completed application for a land disturbance permit 1 an application form available from the city planner the form shall include the berkeley county parcel identification numbers and the address where available of the property proposed for land development 2 an application fee in the amount set by hanahan city council 3 an approved preliminary land development plan or conditionally approved preliminary land development plan that reflects adherence to all planning commission conditions of approval 4 tree protection plans per of the hanahan zoning 5 any vegetation to be preserved for required and otherwise proposed buffering undisturbed green space or other purposes 6 reviewed and approved engineering plans for necessary utilities ie  sewerage potable water electricity street lighting and stormwater drainage proposed to serve the land development the applicant shall be responsible for submitting plans to appropriate agencies for review and approval approvals shall be verified by an official letter from the appropriate agency 7 plans to control erosion and sedimentation to protect water quality and to protect endangered species as approved by state and federal agencies with jurisdiction approval shall be verified by an official letter from the appropriate agency 8 copies of any encroachment permits required by sc department of transportation berkeley county us army corps of engineers and other county state or federal agencies with jurisdiction b documentation requirements the completed application for a land disturbance permit shall meet the following standards 1 engineering plans shall meet the standards of the utility provider expected to accept responsibility for the improvements including sc department of engineering berkeley county engineering berkeley county water and sanitation authority et al 2 engineering plans for improvements proposed for private maintenance shall nevertheless meet documentation requirements promulgated by scdot berkeley county engineering and bcw&sa engineering plans shall then be eligible for thirdparty review per of this ordinance 3 documentation shall be in accordance with the most recent edition of the minimum standards manual for the practice of land surveying in south carolina as promulgated by the laws of south carolina 197 title 40 4 all engineering plans shall include the signature seal and certification of a registered professional land surveyor andor engineer as applicable that the drawings accurately reflect a survey made by him or her that any changes from the description appearing in the last recorded transfer of land contained in the final plat are so indicated that all monuments shown thereon actually exist or will be installed and that their positions are accurately shown 35  final platminor land development plat a application requirements the following constitute a completed application for final maintenance of improvements 41  intent of chapter before the final plat is signed and stamped for approval by the city planner the developer shall either a complete all public improvements as required in this ordinance and dedicate those public improvements to the appropriate body free and clear of all liens and encumbrances on the dedicated property and public improvements  or b ensure completion of all public improvements as required in this ordinance via written signed agreement by financial warranty and dedicate those public improvements to the appropriate body upon completion free and clear of all liens and encumbrances on the dedicated property and public improvements 42  improvements agreement and warranty a the developer shall indicate his desire to guarantee public improvements by submitting a written signed agreement and financial warranty with or prior to a completed application for final plat approval to the city planner b the developer shall sign a written agreement binding him to complete the improvements within two 2 years of final plat approval as indicated by the dated signature of the city planner the final plat shall be referenced in the agreement c the developer shall submit one 1 or a combination of the following financial warranties to the city planner and the written signed agreement with the completed application for final plat approval 1 a nocontest irrevocable bank letter of credit  2 a performance and payment bond underwritten by a corporate surety licensed by the state of south carolina  or 3 a cashiers check or cash equivalent d the financial warranty shall be in an amount equivalent to one hundred fifty 150 percent of the total costs of the public improvements proposed to be ensured the warranty shall name the city of hanahan the beneficiary the city planner shall be authorized to review and approve the costs estimates which may be recommended by a thirdparty professional engineer provided for in of this ordinance e the city planner will forward the agreement and warranty to the city attorney for review and comment the developer shall address those comments and resubmit the agreement if deemed necessary by the city attorney f an agreement and warranty acceptable to the city of hanahan shall be required components of a completed application for final plat approval 43  completion of improvements a if guaranteed public improvements are not completed as required the developer shall be in default the city shall be authorized to utilize funds of the financial warranty to let or relet a contract to complete the improvements any funds remaining from the warranty after successful completion of the improvements shall be returned to the developer b as the developer completes improvements they shall be inspected by the city planner or a thirdparty professional engineer who shall submit a written report to the city planner regarding adherence to the requirements of this ordinance and other applicable standards c the city planner shall review the thirdparty professional engineers report and relay it to the developer who shall address the comments in the report to the satisfaction of the city planner d once the developer has completed the guaranteed public improvements as required he shall prepare record drawings of all improvements which shall conform in all respects to the final plat and reflect guaranteed public improvements as installed the developer shall submit the record drawings to the city planner for review if the record drawing meets the requirements of this ordinance the city planner shall sign and date them approved the developer shall submit the drawing to berkeley county register of deeds e upon successful recordation the city of hanahan shall release the financial warranty to the developer the warranty may be partially released to the developer as improvements are completed in stages at the discretion of the city planner 44  performance of completed improvements to be guaranteed a the developer shall guarantee the performance of completed roads and other improvements proposed to be dedicated to the city of hanahan berkeley county or a property owners association for a period of two 2 years after the improvements are documented and recorded with the berkeley county register of deeds this shall be accomplished via written signed agreement by the developer with a financial warranty which shall be submitted to the city planner b the developer shall submit one 1 or a combination of the following financial warranties to the city planner with the written signed agreement completed application for final plat approval 1 a nocontest irrevocable bank letter of credit  2 a performance and payment bond underwritten by a corporate surety licensed by the state of south carolina  or 3 a cashiers check or cash equivalent c the financial warranty shall be in an amount equivalent to twenty 20 percent of the total costs of the completed guaranteed public improvements the warranty shall name the city of hanahan the beneficiary the city planner shall be authorized to approve the costs stated which may be reviewed by a thirdparty professional engineer provided for in of this ordinance d the city planner will forward the agreement and warranty to the city attorney for review and comment the developer shall address those comments and resubmit the agreement if deemed necessary by the city attorney e if the city planner finds any deficiencies in completed public improvements he shall notify the developer in writing who shall have fifteen 15 days to respond and indicate a time frame to correct the deficiency to the satisfaction of the city planner f if deficiencies in guaranteed public improvements are not rectified as required the developer shall be in default the city shall be authorized to utilize funds of the financial warranty to let or relet a contract to complete the improvements g the financial warranty and performance guarantee for completed public improvements shall expire within two 2 years and any remaining funds shall be returned to the developer 45  maintenance of improvements a the developer shall provide for the perpetual maintenance of all public improvements via one 1 of the following 1 dedication to a public entity equipped to maintain those public improvements offered to it the public entity may accept or refuse the improvements at its sole discretion 2 conveyance of public improvements to a private entity equipped to maintain those public improvements offered to it 3 establishment of a property owners association and conveyance of public improvements thereto the association must be duly chartered by the state of south carolina and recorded with the berkeley county register of deeds b the developer shall provide for the perpetual maintenance environmental resources including open space and wetlands and any associated buffering via one 1 of the aforementioned maintenance vehicles subsections a13 or via one 1 of the following 1 conveyance of the environmental resources to a landowner typically a nonprofit organization whose principal mission is conservation of natural and cultural resources with deed restrictions to that effect  or 2 dedication of a conservation easement protecting the environmental resources to a landowner typically a nonprofit organization whose principal mission is conservation of natural and cultural resources with a legal maintenance agreement from the same c the improvements shall be conveyed with appropriate easements andor deed restrictions that ensure perpetual service of the improvements to the community and public that shall appear on the plat in illustration andor in writing as appropriate the text shall specify the purpose and use of the improvements d a copy of a title insurance policy shall be furnished to the city planner for review by the city attorney indicating that the improvements have been completed are ready for dedication or conveyance to the appropriate body and are free and clear of any and all liens and encumbrances 5  design and improvements standards 51  intent of chapter assurance of completion of improvements is necessary to ensure the performance of installed public improvements to the prospective property owner occupant public and the city of hanahan 52  general standards a conformity improvements shall be installed in accordance with the requirements and standards set forth in this ordinance and other specifications and policies of the city of hanahan berkeley county engineering berkeley county water and sanitation authority charleston water system the south carolina department of transportation the south carolina department of health and environmental control and other agencies of jurisdiction prior to final plat approval and after all applicable permits have been issued by the agencies b access and inspections before beginning any work within the development the developer shall make arrangements with those public agencies charged with the enforcement of the provisions of this ordinance to provide for adequate inspection of the improvements all public agencies shall have access to the premises and structures of a development under jurisdiction of this ordinance during reasonable hours to make those inspections as deemed necessary by them to ensure compliance with the provisions of this ordinance 53  monuments a monuments shall be installed at all angles formed by intersection of lot lines rightofway boundaries and all exterior corners of the development b monuments shall be onequarter 14 inch steel rods or threequarter 34 inch iron pipes not less than twentyfour 24 inches long and shall be placed vertically in the ground so as to extend two 2 inches above finished grade 54  lot boundaries and proportions a the lot size width shape grade and orientation shall be in relation to street and block design existing topographical and natural vegetative conditions and the type of development and use contemplated b the developer shall propose parcel boundaries insofar as practical such that landmark trees and significant groupings of protected trees occur in required yards and do not need to be cleared for building sites c corner lots shall be of sufficient size and shape to permit required building setback and orientation to both streets d the average depth of a lot under two 2 acres in size shall be no more than five 5 times its average width unless it is a doublefrontage lot in which case the average depth shall be no greater than seven 7 times its average width so as to accommodate onsite street parking and loading accessed by an alley in the rear of the lot e the frontage of a lot on a transportation rightofway shall be at least twothirds  23  its average width f a lot shall be at least eighteen 18 feet wide with eighteen 18 feet of frontage on a transportation rightofway ingressegress easement in accordance with individual zoning districts may require wider lots andor more frontage g any remnants of land not meeting lot area width and frontage required by city of hanahan zoning and land development standards shall be incorporated into existing or proposed lots  legally dedicated to public use if acceptable to the city  deeded to an appropriate utility provider to be occupied by infrastructure if acceptable to the provider  or restricted by deed to community use for open space stormwater management or transportation deedrestricted parcels shall be maintained in accordance with infrastructure maintenance procedures set forth in of this ordinance  lot access and orientation the developer shall demonstrate access to all proposed parcels either by frontage on a transportation or ingressegress easement in compliance with one 1 of the following options a the lot shall abut a transportation rightofway or ingressegress easement with a street meeting or exceeding hanahan land development standards b the lot facing a mew or other common area for pedestrian circulation shall abut a transportation rightofway or ingressegress easement with an alley meeting or exceeding hanahan land development standards c the lot shall be oriented directly toward the street insofar as practical side lot lines shall be perpendicular to straight streets or radial to curved streets insofar as practical d the lot shall directly address the street intended to serve it no other property or structure shall partially or wholly intervene between the lot and the street serving the lot flag lots shall be prohibited 55  blocks  block conditions a for the purposes of this ordinance and planning commissions determination of compliance therewith blocks shall be any area defined by two 2 or more linear elements of vehicular circulation providing access to residential or nonresidential units lots offices storefronts etc including roads fire lanes and other drives providing access to and within residential and nonresidential communities including townhouse developments apartment complexes commercial and industrial parks shopping centers mobile home parks and other similar land developments b alleys parking lot aisles and other lanes intended for access to covered or uncovered parking stalls and not relied upon for access to residential or nonresidential units lots offices storefronts etc shall not be considered part of the block perimeter c in the event that vehicular circulation does not constitute the entire perimeter of a block the block shall be considered bounded by adjacent property boundaries andor drainage ways including wetlands for the purpose of considering the size and scale of the block  block design orientation and scale a blocks shall be oriented to complement natural topography so as to minimize need for grading and clearing of natural resources such as trees b blocks shall be oriented to complement natural stormwater drainage patterns and wetlands c blocks shall be sized in proportion to the speed and volume of vehicular and pedestrian traffic expected within those rightsofway or easements defining the block d blocks shall be sized in proportion to existing andor proposed land uses within the block and in proportion to the scale of structures sheltering such land uses e dimensions for blocks may be specified in zoning districts to ensure the existing or intended scale of the district is achieved and enhanced 56  roads  general road standards a roads shall meet or exceed all design and construction standards provided in aashto green book a policy on geometric design of highways and streets 5th edition a publication of the american association of state highway and transportation officials 200 or most recent edition b the city of hanahan accepts no roads for public maintenance meeting or achieving land development standards for roads in hanahan implies no acceptance of such roads for public maintenance the developer seeking to dedicate roads to a public entity shall meet or exceed road standards required by that entity which may differ from or conflict with hanahan standards c the developer may choose to deviate from standards of berkeley county and south carolina department of transportation with good cause as determined by the planning commission the developer shall then propose alternative designs for roads and indicate to the planning commission how the designs further the intent of this ordinance provide better access for all users are more compatible with adjacent existing and proposed land uses andor promote economic development d proposed roads shall be designed to serve all users including truckers automobile drivers bicyclists pedestrians and wheelchair operators where possible conflicts may emerge the road shall be designed for context and proposed use for example road design in industrial areas shall promote truck access whereas road design in neighborhoods shall promote pedestrian access and safety e roads shall be located so as to minimize loss of natural resources including trees and wetlands f proposed road location and design shall account for soils floodplains and other natural conditions and adjust accordingly to ensure the longevity and durability of the road g the proposed road shall remain passable in inclement weather resistant to ponding in travel lanes or flooding in low spots h the proposed road shall not cause flooding or erosive runoff on adjoining parcels i roads shall be constructed to accommodate the type and weight of vehicles routinely expected within the proposed development once it is occupied by permanent users 1 roads in wholesale commercial and industrial areas shall be constructed to accommodate heavytruck traffic generated by the proposed development 2 roads in neighborhood commercial office institutional and residential areas shall be constructed to accommodate private automobile traffic generated by the proposed development 3 alleys serving as secondary access to residences shall accommodate minimal local private automobile traffic and may therefore be constructed with a permeable surface such as gravel coquina or other material that minimizes dust and erosion of the road base 4 all roads except alleys shall be constructed with a hard surface except where the developer can demonstrate specific benefits to the city of hanahan from the construction of permeable surfaces j all roads proposed for construction and improvement shall be equipped with traffic signage consistent with the sc manual on uniform traffic control devices for streets and highways  road system design standards a proposed roads shall be part of a circulation plan within the proposed development and coordinated with the existing road system of the surrounding area b proposed roads shall be integrated into the existing system and where possible provide for the continuation of the road system into adjacent undeveloped high lands for future development such continuations called road tubs shall be dedicated as transportation rightsofway andor easements that allow for use by the traveling public and utilities for future development of the adjacent land road stubs shall be constructed to the same specifications as those for bulk of the road system within the proposed land development c criteria for provision of road stubs 1 the planning commission may require road stubs in any major land development to ensure the possibility of a connection to an adjacent undeveloped tract 2 the commission should require the construction of an existing road stub adjoining a major land development the developer shall be responsible for completing the road system connection by constructing the road in the easement or rightofway provided on adjoining property the constructed road stub shall be integrated into the proposed road system of the major land development 3 the commission should require road stubs to ensure that blocks do not exceed eight hundred 800 feet in length 4 road stubs shall be provided to ensure that no block length exceeds sixteen hundred 1600 feet 5 the planning commission may waive road stub requirements so as not to impose undue hardship on the developer in light of the scale of the proposed land development the commission may further waive this standard where the presence of natural resources or adjacent land use whether current or future make adherence to this standard impractical or undesirable  intersection standards a all roads intersecting other roads shall either intersect directly opposite each other or shall be separated by at least one hundred twentyfive 125 feet from centerline to centerline b all street intersections shall occur at least one hundred twentyfive 125 feet from any railroad rightofway measured from the centerpoint of the intersection perpendicular to the centerline of the railroad rightofway c all roads shall intersect at angles no less than seventyfive 75 degrees unless a traffic circle or movement controls are proposed to prevent awkward or unsafe turning movements d turning movements shall be designed to serve the predominant land uses existing or proposed in the surrounding area pedestrian crossing distances shall be minimized to the greatest extent practical in residential and retail areas turning radii shall be designed to serve truck traffic in industrial areas  singleterminus road standards a proposed permanent singleterminus roads shall be no longer than four hundred 400 feet measured from the centerpoint of its intersection except to provide access to land accessible by no other means due to natural constraints such as wetlands b proposed permanent singleterminus roads shall end in a turnaround at least forty 40 feet in radius the turnaround may have a traversable island of a durable surface and resistant to ponding bounded by a ribbon or mountable curb to ensure the stability and longevity of the adjacent roadway the minimum lane width of a turnaround shall be sixteen 16 feet c proposed temporary singleterminus roads providing access to future phases of the same proposed land development or to an adjacent developable tract shall be equipped with either a turnaround specified above or a hammerhead that enables emergency and service vehicles to perform a threepoint turn d proposed singleterminus alleys shall be equipped with a turnaround or a hammerhead e no turnaround or hammerhead feature is required for a temporary singleterminus road provided that such road is less than two hundred 200 feet long and that provides no access to a lot  existing roads a to avoid undue hardship on small landowners and prospective homeowners a preexisting road need not be upgraded to meet current standards for a land development that is in all other respects a minor land development as defined by this ordinance b a major land development relying upon a preexisting substandard road shall upgrade the road as practical the planning commission shall determine the extent of upgrades required in its review of the major land development based on the findings of a traffic study as set forth in a cost estimate of upgrades recommended in the study  standards by road type type target speed through leftturn lanes continuous lane width typical curb radius parking drainage 1 sidewalks width 2 alley 1015 mph 120 912 feet 1020 feet
